The execution flow starts when the scheduler's `Run()` method triggers `schedulePeriodic()`, which then invokes the alert rule's `Run()` method to begin evaluation cycles.\n\nDuring evaluation, the rule calls `evalFactory.Create()` and `ConditionEvaluator.Evaluate()` to assess conditions, then passes results to the state manager's `ProcessEvalResults()` for state transitions. Overview\\nGrafana's unified alerting system (ngalert) evaluates alert rules on a schedule and dispatches fired alerts through notification receivers. The flow consists of four main components: rule scheduling, rule evaluation, state management, and notification dispatch.\\n\\n### Rule Scheduler\\n**File:** `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go`\\n\\nThe scheduler is the entry point that orchestrates periodic evaluation of alert rules. Key functions:\\n- `Run(ctx context.Context)`: Starts the scheduler, initializes a ticker, and enters the main evaluation loop\\n- `schedulePeriodic(ctx context.Context, t *ticker.T)`: Main loop that:\\n  - Tracks which alert rules are scheduled for evaluation\\n  - Fetches alert rules from the rules store periodically\\n  - Sends evaluation signals to individual alert rule routines\\n  - Handles rule additions, deletions, and updates\\n  - Uses retry configuration for resilience\\n\\nThe scheduler maintains a rule registry where each alert rule has its own dedicated goroutine for execution.\\n\\n### Alert Rule Evaluation\\n**File:** `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go`\\n\\nEach alert rule runs in its own goroutine orchestrated by the `alertRule` struct. Key functions:\\n\\n- `newAlertRule()`: Factory function that creates an alert rule with state manager, evaluator factory, and sender dependencies\\n\\n- `Run()`: Main loop for an individual alert rule that:\\n  - Receives evaluation signals via a channel (`evalCh`)\\n  - Receives update signals to change rule configuration (`updateCh`)\\n  - Handles rule state resets when updated or paused\\n  - Implements exponential backoff retry logic\\n  - Delegates to `evaluate()` for actual evaluation\\n\\n- `Eval(eval *Evaluation)`: Signals the rule to perform evaluation by sending to `evalCh`\\n\\n- `evaluate(ctx, e *Evaluation, span, shouldRetry, logger)`: Core evaluation logic that:\\n  - Creates a new evaluator from the factory for the rule's condition\\n  - Calls `ruleEval.Evaluate()` to execute queries/expressions\\n  - Measures evaluation duration and tracks metrics\\n  - Calls `stateManager.ProcessEvalResults()` with evaluation results and a callback to send alerts\\n  - Implements retry logic with exponential backoff\\n\\n- `send(ctx, logger, states StateTransitions)`: Converts state transitions to PostableAlerts and calls `sender.Send()`\\n\\n- `expireAndSend(ctx, states)`: Sends resolved alerts when rules are deleted or updated\\n\\n### Evaluation Engine\\n**File:** `pkg/services/ngalert/eval/eval.go`\\n\\nThe evaluator executes the rule's query/expression condition. Key components:\\n\\n- `EvaluatorFactory`: Interface with `Create()` method that builds evaluators for rule conditions\\n\\n- `NewEvaluatorFactory()`: Creates the evaluator factory, configured with evaluation timeout and result limits\\n\\n- `ConditionEvaluator`: Interface with:\\n  - `Evaluate(ctx, now time.Time)`: Evaluates condition and returns typed Results\\n  - `EvaluateRaw(ctx, now time.Time)`: Returns raw backend response\\n\\n- `EvaluateAlert()`: Converts backend query response to alert instance states (determined by alert values, thresholds, and evaluation time)\\n\\n### State Management and Transitions\\n**File:** `pkg/services/ngalert/state/manager.go`\\n\\nManages alert instance state and determines which alerts to send to notification receivers:\\n\\n- `Manager`: Core state management component that:\\n  - Caches alert instance states per rule\\n  - Persists state to database\\n  - Coordinates with historian for audit trail\\n\\n- `ProcessEvalResults(ctx, evaluatedAt time.Time, alertRule, results, extraLabels, send Sender)`: Main method that:\\n  - Calls `setNextStateForRule()` to compute state transitions based on evaluation results\\n  - Handles NoData and Error states based on rule configuration\\n  - Processes missing series (firing alerts with no data in current evaluation)\\n  - Calls `updateLastSentAt()` to determine which states should be sent\\n  - Persists all state changes (both sent and unsent)\\n  - Records state transitions in historian\\n  - Invokes the `send` callback with state transitions to send\\n\\n- `setNextStateForRule()`: Determines new states for each alert instance based on:\\n  - Evaluation results and thresholds\\n  - Previous state of the alert instance\\n  - Pending duration (time alert must breach threshold before firing)\\n  - NoDataState and ExecutionErrorState rule configuration\\n\\n- `updateLastSentAt()`: Filters state transitions to identify which should be sent based on:\\n  - State changes (e.g., firing to normal)\\n  - Resend delay (30 seconds by default)\\n  - Resolved alert retention period\\n\\n- `DeleteStateByRuleUID()`: Removes all instances of a rule and creates resolved state transitions for firing alerts\\n\\n### Alert Notification Dispatch\\n**File:** `pkg/services/ngalert/sender/router.go`\\n\\nRoutes alerts to internal and/or external Alertmanagers:\\n\\n- `AlertsRouter`: Handles alert routing based on organization configuration. Key functions:\\n  - `NewAlertsRouter()`: Creates router with dependencies on multi-org alertmanager and external alertmanager configuration\\n  - `Send(ctx, key AlertRuleKey, alerts PostableAlerts)`: Main dispatch function that:\\n    - Checks if organization is configured for internal, external, or both alertmanagers\\n    - Gets org's alertmanager from `multiOrgNotifier.AlertmanagerFor()`\\n    - Calls `PutAlerts()` on the alertmanager\\n    - Sends to external alertmanagers if configured via `ExternalAlertmanager.SendAlerts()`\\n    - Broadcasts alerts to cluster peers if enabled\\n  - `SyncAndApplyConfigFromDatabase()`: Periodically syncs alertmanager configuration from database\\n  - Maintains list of external alertmanagers per organization\\n\\n### Multi-Org Alertmanager\\n**File:** `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go`\\n\\nManages separate Alertmanager instances per Grafana organization:\\n\\n- `MultiOrgAlertmanager`: Container for organization-specific alertmanagers. Key functions:\\n  - `NewMultiOrgAlertmanager()`: Factory that:\\n    - Sets up clustering if configured (Redis for HA)\\n    - Initializes per-org alertmanager factory\\n    - Configures alert broadcast channel for cluster communication\\n  - `AlertmanagerFor(orgID)`: Returns or creates alertmanager for given organization\\n  - Creates per-org Alertmanager instances on demand with isolation\\n\\n### Internal Alertmanager (Per-Organization)\\n**File:** `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/alertmanager.go`\\n\\nHandles notification delivery and routing for a single organization:\\n\\n- `alertmanager`: Wraps the core `GrafanaAlertmanager` from the alerting library. Key functions:\\n  - `NewAlertmanager()`: Creates org-specific alertmanager that:\\n    - Initializes state stores for silences and notification logs\\n    - Sets up maintenance options for periodic garbage collection\\n    - Loads persisted silence and notification log state\\n    - Configures dispatch timer (async or sync)\\n  - `PutAlerts(ctx, postableAlerts)`: Receives alerts and:\\n    - Converts Grafana alert models to alerting library models\\n    - Calls `Base.PutAlerts()` on the wrapped `GrafanaAlertmanager`\\n    - This sends alerts through the Alertmanager's dispatch pipeline to receivers/integrations\\n\\n### Service Integration\\n**File:** `pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go`\\n\\nWires up all components:\\n- Creates and initializes the scheduler\\n- Creates state manager with persistence layer\\n- Creates evaluator factory\\n- Creates alerts router\\n- Creates multi-org alertmanager\\n- Coordinates lifecycle of all services\\n\\n### Complete Call Chain\\n\\n1. **Scheduler calls `Eval()`\\n4. **Evaluation Execution**: `evaluate()` → `evalFactory.Create()` → `ConditionEvaluator.Evaluate()` → `EvaluateAlert()`\\n5. **State Processing**: `stateManager.ProcessEvalResults()` Overview\\nGrafana's unified alerting system (ngalert) evaluates alert rules on a schedule and dispatches fired alerts through notification receivers. The flow consists of four main components: rule scheduling, rule evaluation, state management, and notification dispatch.\\n\\n### Rule Scheduler\\n**File:** `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go`\\n\\nThe scheduler is the entry point that orchestrates periodic evaluation of alert rules. Key functions:\\n- `Run(ctx context.Context)`: Starts the scheduler, initializes a ticker, and enters the main evaluation loop\\n- `schedulePeriodic(ctx context.Context, t *ticker.T)`: Main loop that:\\n  - Tracks which alert rules are scheduled for evaluation\\n  - Fetches alert rules from the rules store periodically\\n  - Sends evaluation signals to individual alert rule routines\\n  - Handles rule additions, deletions, and updates\\n  - Uses retry configuration for resilience\\n\\nThe scheduler maintains a rule registry where each alert rule has its own dedicated goroutine for execution.\\n\\n### Alert Rule Evaluation\\n**File:** `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go`\\n\\nEach alert rule runs in its own goroutine orchestrated by the `alertRule` struct. Key functions:\\n\\n- `newAlertRule()`: Factory function that creates an alert rule with state manager, evaluator factory, and sender dependencies\\n\\n- `Run()`: Main loop for an individual alert rule that:\\n  - Receives evaluation signals via a channel (`evalCh`)\\n  - Receives update signals to change rule configuration (`updateCh`)\\n  - Handles rule state resets when updated or paused\\n  - Implements exponential backoff retry logic\\n  - Delegates to `evaluate()` for actual evaluation\\n\\n- `Eval(eval *Evaluation)`: Signals the rule to perform evaluation by sending to `evalCh`\\n\\n- `evaluate(ctx, e *Evaluation, span, shouldRetry, logger)`: Core evaluation logic that:\\n  - Creates a new evaluator from the factory for the rule's condition\\n  - Calls `ruleEval.Evaluate()` to execute queries/expressions\\n  - Measures evaluation duration and tracks metrics\\n  - Calls `stateManager.ProcessEvalResults()` with evaluation results and a callback to send alerts\\n  - Implements retry logic with exponential backoff\\n\\n- `send(ctx, logger, states StateTransitions)`: Converts state transitions to PostableAlerts and calls `sender.Send()`\\n\\n- `expireAndSend(ctx, states)`: Sends resolved alerts when rules are deleted or updated\\n\\n### Evaluation Engine\\n**File:** `pkg/services/ngalert/eval/eval.go`\\n\\nThe evaluator executes the rule's query/expression condition. Key components:\\n\\n- `EvaluatorFactory`: Interface with `Create()` method that builds evaluators for rule conditions\\n\\n- `NewEvaluatorFactory()`: Creates the evaluator factory, configured with evaluation timeout and result limits\\n\\n- `ConditionEvaluator`: Interface with:\\n  - `Evaluate(ctx, now time.Time)`: Evaluates condition and returns typed Results\\n  - `EvaluateRaw(ctx, now time.Time)`: Returns raw backend response\\n\\n- `EvaluateAlert()`: Converts backend query response to alert instance states (determined by alert values, thresholds, and evaluation time)\\n\\n### State Management and Transitions\\n**File:** `pkg/services/ngalert/state/manager.go`\\n\\nManages alert instance state and determines which alerts to send to notification receivers:\\n\\n- `Manager`: Core state management component that:\\n  - Caches alert instance states per rule\\n  - Persists state to database\\n  - Coordinates with historian for audit trail\\n\\n- `ProcessEvalResults(ctx, evaluatedAt time.Time, alertRule, results, extraLabels, send Sender)`: Main method that:\\n  - Calls `setNextStateForRule()` to compute state transitions based on evaluation results\\n  - Handles NoData and Error states based on rule configuration\\n  - Processes missing series (firing alerts with no data in current evaluation)\\n  - Calls `updateLastSentAt()` to determine which states should be sent\\n  - Persists all state changes (both sent and unsent)\\n  - Records state transitions in historian\\n  - Invokes the `send` callback with state transitions to send\\n\\n- `setNextStateForRule()`: Determines new states for each alert instance based on:\\n  - Evaluation results and thresholds\\n  - Previous state of the alert instance\\n  - Pending duration (time alert must breach threshold before firing)\\n  - NoDataState and ExecutionErrorState rule configuration\\n\\n- `updateLastSentAt()`: Filters state transitions to identify which should be sent based on:\\n  - State changes (e.g., firing to normal)\\n  - Resend delay (30 seconds by default)\\n  - Resolved alert retention period\\n\\n- `DeleteStateByRuleUID()`: Removes all instances of a rule and creates resolved state transitions for firing alerts\\n\\n### Alert Notification Dispatch\\n**File:** `pkg/services/ngalert/sender/router.go`\\n\\nRoutes alerts to internal and/or external Alertmanagers:\\n\\n- `AlertsRouter`: Handles alert routing based on organization configuration. Key functions:\\n  - `NewAlertsRouter()`: Creates router with dependencies on multi-org alertmanager and external alertmanager configuration\\n  - `Send(ctx, key AlertRuleKey, alerts PostableAlerts)`: Main dispatch function that:\\n    - Checks if organization is configured for internal, external, or both alertmanagers\\n    - Gets org's alertmanager from `multiOrgNotifier.AlertmanagerFor()`\\n    - Calls `PutAlerts()` on the alertmanager\\n    - Sends to external alertmanagers if configured via `ExternalAlertmanager.SendAlerts()`\\n    - Broadcasts alerts to cluster peers if enabled\\n  - `SyncAndApplyConfigFromDatabase()`: Periodically syncs alertmanager configuration from database\\n  - Maintains list of external alertmanagers per organization\\n\\n### Multi-Org Alertmanager\\n**File:** `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go`\\n\\nManages separate Alertmanager instances per Grafana organization:\\n\\n- `MultiOrgAlertmanager`: Container for organization-specific alertmanagers. Key functions:\\n  - `NewMultiOrgAlertmanager()`: Factory that:\\n    - Sets up clustering if configured (Redis for HA)\\n    - Initializes per-org alertmanager factory\\n    - Configures alert broadcast channel for cluster communication\\n  - `AlertmanagerFor(orgID)`: Returns or creates alertmanager for given organization\\n  - Creates per-org Alertmanager instances on demand with isolation\\n\\n### Internal Alertmanager (Per-Organization)\\n**File:** `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/alertmanager.go`\\n\\nHandles notification delivery and routing for a single organization:\\n\\n- `alertmanager`: Wraps the core `GrafanaAlertmanager` from the alerting library. Key functions:\\n  - `NewAlertmanager()`: Creates org-specific alertmanager that:\\n    - Initializes state stores for silences and notification logs\\n    - Sets up maintenance options for periodic garbage collection\\n    - Loads persisted silence and notification log state\\n    - Configures dispatch timer (async or sync)\\n  - `PutAlerts(ctx, postableAlerts)`: Receives alerts and:\\n    - Converts Grafana alert models to alerting library models\\n    - Calls `Base.PutAlerts()` on the wrapped `GrafanaAlertmanager`\\n    - This sends alerts through the Alertmanager's dispatch pipeline to receivers/integrations\\n\\n### Service Integration\\n**File:** `pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go`\\n\\nWires up all components:\\n- Creates and initializes the scheduler\\n- Creates state manager with persistence layer\\n- Creates evaluator factory\\n- Creates alerts router\\n- Creates multi-org alertmanager\\n- Coordinates lifecycle of all services\\n\\n### Complete Call Chain\\n\\n1. **Scheduler Start**: `schedule.Run()` → `schedulePeriodic()`\\n2. **Rule Evaluation Signal**: Scheduler sends eval signal to alert rule's channel\\n3. **Rule Processing**: `alertRule.Run()` receives signal → calls `Eval()`\\n4. **Evaluation Execution**: `evaluate()` → `evalFactory.Create()` → `ConditionEvaluator.Evaluate()` → `EvaluateAlert()`\\n5. **State Processing**: `stateManager.ProcessEvalResults()` → `setNextStateForRule()` → `updateLastSentAt()`\\n6. **Alert Dispatch**: Callback invokes `alertRule.send()` → `AlertsRouter.Send()`\\n7. **Routing to Alertmanager**: `AlertsRouter.Send()` → `MultiOrgAlertmanager.AlertmanagerFor()` → org's `Alertmanager.PutAlerts()`\\n8. **Notification Delivery**: `Alertmanager.PutAlerts()` → `GrafanaAlertmanager.PutAlerts()` → dispatcher sends to receivers/integrations\\n\\nThis modular architecture allows for:\\n- Per-organization isolation via MultiOrgAlertmanager\\n- Flexible routing (internal/external alertmanagers)\\n- Proper state tracking and notification deduplication\\n- Resilience with retry logic and state persistence\\n- Clustering support for high availability\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

runs in its own goroutine, receives evaluation signals, and manages retry logic\n\n3. **Evaluation Engine** (`eval/eval.go`): Executes rule queries/expressions using the expression service to produce metric results\n\n4. **State Manager** (`state/manager.go`): Processes evaluation results, determines state transitions, and decides which alerts to send based on thresholds and timing\n\n5. **Alerts Router** (`sender/router.go`): Routes alerts to internal Alertmanager and/or external Alertmanagers based on organization configuration\n\n6. **Multi-Org Alertmanager** (`notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go`): Maintains per-organization Alertmanager instances for isolation\n\n7. **Internal Alertmanager** (`notifier/alertmanager.go`): Receives alerts and dispatches them through the notification routing engine to receivers/integrations\n\n### Complete Flow:\nScheduler → Rule Evaluation → Query Execution → State Calculation → Alert Decision → Router → Org Alertmanager → Receivers\n\nThe answer file includes all relevant files, key symbols, the complete call chain, and detailed narrative documentation at
